## Diagram 3

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
  [*] --> Idle
  Idle --> Parsing : run main(argv)
  Parsing --> Configuring
  Configuring --> EnvRead
  EnvRead --> OAuthCall
  OAuthCall --> TokenStored
  TokenStored --> RemoveExisting
  RemoveExisting --> CreatingShipment
  CreatingShipment --> Validating
  Validating --> Cleanup
  Cleanup --> [*]
```
